<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пугать.html>пуга́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pugátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ло</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пугать.html>пу́гало</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">púgalo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пугать.html>пу́гала</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пугать.html>пу́гала</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пугать.html>пу́гал</a></b>)
</p>

<li>bugaboo, bugbear</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> fright</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пугать.html>пуга́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pugátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:испугать.html>испуга́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:напугать.html>напуга́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пугнуть.html>пугну́ть</a></b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуговица.html>пу́говица</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">púgovica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуговица.html>пу́говицы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуговица.html>пу́говицы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуговица.html>пу́говиц</a></b>)

***пуд.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пуд.html>пуд</a> (9968)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pǫdъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pondo</i>, from Classical <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pondus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуд.html>пуд</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pud</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуд.html>пу́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуд.html>пуды́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пуд.html>пудо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pood (an obsolete Russian unit of mass equal to 40 <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фунт.html>фунт</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">funt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or 16.3804815 kg (36.1127 pounds))</li>
<li>pood (in modern kettlebells, rounded off to 16 kg (35.2739 pounds))</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> percent

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пук.html>пук</a> (29836)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">пукъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pukŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pǫkъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*pank-</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:пук.html>пук</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">puk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">puk</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">рęk</i>.
</p><p>Further cognates, per Vasmer, are <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">پنگ</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pang</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">date palm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pānus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">millet ear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пук.html>пук</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">puk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пук.html>пу́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пук.html>пуки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пук.html>пуко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>wisp, bunch, bundle, tuft</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пулеметчик.html>пулемётчик</a> (9430)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***пульс.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пульс.html>пульс</a> (5939)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пульс.html>пульс</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pulʹs</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пульс.html>пу́льса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пульс.html>пу́льсы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пульс.html>пу́льсов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pulse (regular beat caused by the heart)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пульсация.html>пульса́ция</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pulʹsácija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пульсировать.html>пульси́ровать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pulʹsírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пульс.html>пульс</a></b>

***пульсировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пульсировать.html>пульси́ровать</a> (10629)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пульсировать.html>пульси́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pulʹsírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to pulsate</li>
<li>to beat, to throb</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

Зализняка — 2a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-пульс-</b>; интерфикс: <b>-ир-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ова</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Pult</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pulpitum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">platform, scaffold</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пульт.html>пульт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pulʹt</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пульт.html>пу́льта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пульт.html>пу́льты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пульт.html>пу́льтов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lectern, music stand
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дирижерский.html>дирижёрский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пульт.html>пульт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dirižórskij pulʹt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">conductor's stand</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>console, (control) panel, benchboard</li>
<li>remote control</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пуля.html>пу́ля</a> (1308)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Either from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kula</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, influenced by <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палить.html>пали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">palítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fire, to burn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пу́шка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">púška</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:куль.html>ку́ля</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kúlja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span
